   'grimādhyāye vyākhyāsyante | bhaktā eva hares tattva-vido māyāṃ taranti,	agrima-aDyAye vyAKyAsyante | BaktAH eva hareH tattva-vidaH mAyAm taranti,
   te coktāḥ ṣaḍ-vidhā atrety adhyāyārtho nirūpitaḥ ||30||	te ca-uktAH zax-viDAH atra-iti aDyAya-arTaH nirUpitaH ||30||
   iti sārārtha-varṣiṇyāṃ harṣiṇyāṃ bhakta-cetasām |	iti sAra-arTa-varziNyAm harziNyAm Bakta--cetasAm |
   gītāsu saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ saṅgataḥ saṅgataḥ satām ||7||	gItAsu saptamaH aDyAyaH saFgataH saFgataH satAm ||7||
   baladevaḥ - na ca tat-sevayā prāptaṃ taj-jñānaṃ kadācid api bhraṃśety āha	baladevaH  na ca tat-sevayA prAptam tat--jQAnam kadAcid api BraMSa-iti Aha
   sādhīti | adhibhūtenādhidaivenādhiyajñena ca sahitaṃ māṃ ye viduḥ	sADi-iti | aDiBUtena-aDidEvena-aDiyajQena ca sahitam mAm ye viduH
   sat-prasaṅgāj jānanti, te prayāṇa-kāle mṛtyu-samaye 'pi māṃ vidur na tu	sat--prasaFgAt jAnanti, te prayANa--kAle mRtyu--samaye api mAm viduH na tu
   tad-anyavad vyagrāḥ santo māṃ vismarantīty arthaḥ ||30||	tat--anya-vat vyagrAH santaH mAm vismaranti-iti arTaH ||30||
   māṃ vidus tattvato bhaktā man-māyām uttaranti te |	mAm viduH tattvataH BaktAH man-mAyAm uttaranti te |
   te punaḥ pañcadhety eṣa saptamasya vinirṇayaḥ ||	te punar paQcaDA-iti eza saptamasya vinirNayaH ||
   iti śrīmad-bhagavad-gītopaniṣad-bhāṣye saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ |	iti SrI-mat--Bagavat--gIta-upanizad--BAzye saptamaH aDyAyaH |
